translateY(-3px);
    box-shadow: 0 10px 20px rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.2);
  }

  &:active {
    transform: translateY(-1px);
    box-shadow: 0 5px 10px rgba(0, 0, 0, 0
```

    box-shadow: 0 10px 20px rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.2);
  }

  &:active {
    transform: translateY(-1px);
    box-shadow: 0 5px 10px rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.2);
  }

  &::after {
    content: "";
    display: inline-block;
    height: 100%;
    width:
```

    box-shadow: 0 10px 20px rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.2);
  }

  &:active {
    transform: translateY(-1px);
    box-shadow: 0 5px 10px rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.2);
  }

  &::after {
    content: "";
    display: inline-block;
    height: 100%;
    width: 100%;
   
```

    box-shadow: 0 10px 20px rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.2);
  }

  &:active {
    transform: translateY(-1px);
    box-shadow: 0 5px 10px rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.2);
  }

  &::after {
    content: "";
    display: inline-block;
    height: 100%;
    width: 100%;
    border-radius: 100px;
    position: absolute;
    top: 0;
    left: 0;
    z-index
```

  &::after {
    content: "";
    display: inline-block;
    height: 100%;
    width: 100%;
    border-radius: 100px;
    position: absolute;
    top: 0;
    left: 0;
    z-index: -1;

```

    box-shadow: 0 5px 10px rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.2);
  }

  &::after {
    content: "";
    display: inline-block;
    height: 100%;
    width: 100%;
    border-radius: 100px;
    position: absolute;
    top: 0;
    left: 0;
    z-index: -1;
    transition: all 0.4s;
    background-color: #
```

    box-shadow: 0 10px 20px rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.2);
  }

  &:active {
    transform: translateY(-1px);
    box-shadow: 0 5px 10px rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.2);
  }

  &::after {
    content: "";
    display: inline-block;
    height: 100%;
    width: 100%;
    border-radius: 100px;
    position: absolute;
    top: 0;
    left: 0;
    z-index: -1;
    transition: all 0.4s;
    background-color: #fff;
  }


```

    box-shadow: 0 10px 20px rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.2);
  }

  &:active {
    transform: translateY(-1px);
    box-shadow: 0 5px 10px rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.2);
  }

  &::after {
    content: "";
    display: inline-block;
    height: 100%;
    width: 100%;
    border-radius: 100px;
    position: absolute;
    top: 0;
    left: 0;
    z-index: -1;
    transition: all 0.4s;
    background-color: #fff;
  }

  &:hover
```

    box-shadow: 0 5px 10px rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.2);
  }

  &::after {
    content: "";
    display: inline-block;
    height: 100%;
    width: 100%;
    border-radius: 100px;
    position: absolute;
    top: 0;
    left: 0;
    z-index: -1;
    transition: all 0.4s;
    background-color: #fff;
  }

  &:hover::after {
    transform: scale
```

    top: 0;
    left: 0;
    z-index: -1;
    transition: all 0.4s;
    background-color: #fff;
  }

  &:hover::after {
    transform: scaleX(1.4) scale
```

    transform: translateY(-1px);
    box-shadow: 0 5px 10px rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.2);
  }

  &::after {
    content: "";
    display: inline-block;
    height: 100%;
    width: 100%;
    border-radius: 100px;
    position: absolute;
    top: 0;
    left: 0;
    z-index: -1;
    transition: all 0.4s;
    background-color: #fff;
  }

  &:hover::after {
    transform: scaleX(1.4) scaleY(1
```

    width: 100%;
    border-radius: 100px;
    position: absolute;
    top: 0;
    left: 0;
    z-index: -1;
    transition: all 0.4s;
    background-color: #fff;
  }

  &:hover::after {
    transform: scaleX(1.4) scaleY(1.6);
   
```

    box-shadow: 0 5px 10px rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.2);
  }

  &::after {
    content: "";
    display: inline-block;
    height: 100%;
    width: 100%;
    border-radius: 100px;
    position: absolute;
    top: 0;
    left: 0;
    z-index: -1;
    transition: all 0.4s;
    background-color: #fff;
  }

  &:hover::after {
    transform: scaleX(1.4) scaleY(1.6);
    opacity: 
```
